# Active Runs Ledger

Coordination surface for CLIs (Claude Code agents, manual sessions, skill
invocations) operating concurrently on this checkout. Each session that
materially edits the working tree should touch this file twice:

1. **At session start (Phase 0):** read this file, scan `## Active

### byom-mixed-engine ŌĆö mixed engine (Claude orchestrator + local Ollama llm_delegate tool) (session 7c484b45)
- Started: 2026-06-11 ~17:15. Completed: 2026-06-11 ~18:50. Commits: 428718b05 (backend), d758e2900 (frontend toggle + lfm2.5 catalog), 2d3d8eb87 (feature doc) + findings commit.
- Paths: mcp_server/tools.rs (llm_delegate), engine/cli_mcp_config.rs, engine/runner/mod.rs, settings_keys.rs, sub_use_cases detail panel, en.json, docs/plans/mixed-engine-byom.md.
- Note: live-verified AŌĆōF runs incl. organic delegation + graceful Ollama-death recovery + memory-poisoning finding. Verdict: resilience-proven architecture, not a cost lever; v2 = replace headless cli_text calls via ByomPolicy Simple routing. Bench personas "Engine Bench"/"Engine Bench Bulk" kept in DB for output inspection.

` for
   running entries. If any entry's declared paths overlap with this
   session's planned scope AND the entry is less than 2 hours old AND its
   status is `started`, surface the conflict to the user before proceeding
   (options: abort, coordinate, or proceed-with-awareness). Then append
   your own entry under `## Active`.
2. **At session end (Phase 11/13):** move your `## Active` entry to the
   top of `## Recently completed

   <sha>)` or `aborted (<reason>)`. Trim entries older than 14 days from
   `## Recently completed`.

If your session crashes, your entry stays under `## Active` with a stale
timestamp ŌĆö the next session can recognize it as abandoned.

## Conventions

- Timestamps are local time, format `YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`.
- `Paths` declares the directories or globs the session expects to read or
  write. Be specific enough that overlap is meaningful (`src/features/agents/sub_chat/`
  is good; `src/` is too broad to be useful).
- The `## Active` section is the source of truth; `## Recently completed`
  is a rolling history window.
- Concurrent edits to this file: re-read on Edit failure, repeat the
  conflict check, retry. The Edit tool's unique-old-string rule prevents
  silent clobbers.

  - **Status:** in progress ŌĆö tsc clean, eslint 0 on touched files. Chat width 350px confirmed OK by user.
    - FLICKER ROOT CAUSE (corrected): NOT the ContentHeader. It's the app-wide background **grid layer** at `PersonasPage.tsx:271` ŌĆö a full-screen `absolute inset-0` CSS `repeating-linear-gradient` of 1px blue lines (32px cells) behind all content (`z-10`). The layer isn't GPU-isolated, so it shares a paint layer with hover-repainting content; every pointer-move re-rasterizes the gradient, and at fractional Windows DPI a 1px line maps to non-integer device px ŌåÆ shimmer, worst at top/right edges. Fix: `transform-gpu backface-hidden` on the grid + fade layers ŌåÆ one-time raster, composite-only thereafter. Earlier `min-w-[80vw]`ŌåÆ`w-full` guess was WRONG (only narrowed the header) and was reverted.
  - **Branch:** master
  - **Note:** Path-disjoint from active sessions (overview-batch=overview/home-widgets, density=globals.css/themeStore, athena-tour=onboarding). transform-gpu is a light 2D layer promotion, unlike the backdrop-blur previously removed from this same block for the ARM64 compositor freeze. Awaiting user HMR confirmation; fallbacks if it persists: pre-rasterized SVG data-URI grid, or edge-mask to drop the top/right boundary lines.

- **[2026-05-24 ŌĆö completed (commit: 288176ac1)] idea-8ea8d796 ŌĆö WCAG AA contrast audit of muted & tinted text**
  - **What:** Token-level a11y fix. `--muted` (text color ~170├Ś) was sub-AA against the canvas in most dark themes (1.8ŌĆō3.3:1) and `light` (4.48); opacity-tinted `text-muted-foreground/{40-70}` captions fell below AA on light themes. - **[2026-05-24 ŌĆö completed (commits: 7bb31ca6d, merge 8710dcfff)] idea-330cd93f ŌĆö self-scaling RelativeTime primitive with shared ticker**
  - **Source:** Idea requirement (ui_perfectionist). Dozens of relative-time labels each spun their own `setInterval` (PeerList 15s, RelativeTime 15s, rotation ticker 60s), wasting wake-ups, drifting out of sync, and showing stale labels up to 15s past a boundary.
  - **Shipped:** New `src/hooks/utility/timing/relativeTimeTicker.ts` ŌĆö a single app-wide ticker. `useRelativeTimeTick(ts)` derives cadence from a label's age (1s sub-minute, 30s sub-hour, 5m beyond); `useFixedTicker(ms)` subscribes at a constant cadence. The ticker runs at the finest cadence any live subscriber needs and re-renders all of them on one tick (auto-stops when empty). Migrated: `RelativeTime` primitive (was local 15s interval ŌĆö every `<RelativeTime>` app-wide now benefits), `PeerList` (dropped ad-hoc `useRelativeTime` hook), `ExecutionListRow` mobile card (static `formatRelativeTime()` ŌåÆ live `<RelativeTime>`), `useRotationTicker` (credential countdown now coalesces onto the shared ticker). 12 new unit tests.
  - **Paths:** `src/hooks/utility/timing/relativeTimeTicker.ts` (+`__tests__/`), `src/features/shared/components/display/RelativeTime.tsx`, `src/features/sharing/components/PeerList.tsx`, `src/features/agents/sub_executions/components/list/ExecutionListRow.tsx`, `src/features/vault/shared/hooks/useRotationTicker.ts`
  - **Branch:** `worktree-relativetime-prim` (merged no-ff `8710dcfff`, worktree + branch removed).

- **[2026-05-24 ŌĆö completed (commits: 31ead17ac merge, cedc71d4f)] idea-165dceff ŌĆö disabled-control reason tooltips surface on hover + keyboard**
  - **Source:** Idea requirement (ui_perfectionist). `Button` already had a `disabledReason` prop, but the implementation relied on a native disabled `<button>` (which cannot take focus and swallows pointer events) wrapped by a `display:contents` Tooltip span ŌĆö so the reason never reliably surfaced on hover OR keyboard focus.

Added `Button.test.tsx` (4 tests, plain matchers so it's tsc-checked while co-located).

- **[2026-05-14 12:30 ŌåÆ 13:15] ort-arm64-fix ŌĆö predev cache-override for pyke's mislabeled aarch64 tarball**
  - **Status:** completed (commit `93073a8c2` on master).
  - **Source:** in-session user request after `npm run tauri:dev` failed on arm64 Snapdragon X Elite (X1E78100) with `lld-link: error: machine type x64 conflicts with arm64` for `libort_sys-ddea945a6dca0f73.rlib`. `clean:ort` was tried first and did not help ŌĆö the next download produced the same broken bytes, because the SHA256 in `ort-sys-2.0.0-rc.9/dist.txt` is the hash of the mislabeled tarball itself, not of what should be inside.
  - **Root cause:** `ort-sys 2.0.0-rc.9` dist.txt line 8 maps `aarch64-pc-windows-msvc` to `parcel.pyke.io/.../ortrs_static-v1.20.0-aarch64-pc-windows-msvc.tgz` SHA256 `C09BFF5582BCA2EC583E49A32E7B1B406AC930CB18791C3165E82B53516C27DE`. The tarball is named arm64 and hashes correctly; `dumpbin /HEADERS` of the extracted `onnxruntime.lib` reports `8664 machine (x64)`. Confirmed upstream defect, not stale cache. `fastembed 4.9.1` pins both `ort = "=2.0.0-rc.9"` and `ort-sys = "=2.0.0-rc.9"`, so escape via version bump requires a major dep upgrade (fastembed 5.x + ort rc.12) with API risk and no guarantee the upstream is fixed.
  - **Paths shipped (commit `93073a8c2`):**
    - `scripts/ensure-ort-cache.mjs` (NEW, ~416 lines) ŌĆö sniffs cached `onnxruntime.lib`'s actual COFF machine field, downloads Microsoft's official ORT 1.20.0 from `github.com/microsoft/onnxruntime/releases/download/v1.20.0/onnxruntime-win-<arch>-1.20.0.zip` and places it into pyke's expected cache slot when the cache is missing/wrong; tracks state via `.personas-ort-fix-applied` sentinel; evicts stale `libort_sys-*.rlib` from `target/<profile>/deps/` when it predates the sentinel (mtime comparison) so cargo's incremental compile rebuilds it.
    - `package.json` ŌĆö added `ensure:ort-cache` alias + `pretauri:dev` / `pretauri:dev:stable` / `pretauri:dev:test:full` / `pretauri:build` / `pretauri:build:stable` lifecycle hooks. Lite variants skipped (don't compile `ml`).
    - `.claude/CLAUDE.md` ŌĆö added "Picking dev variants ŌĆö when to use lite vs full" decision table and "When builds get slow or break" recovery section.
    - `docs/development/build.md` ŌĆö replaced obsolete "Known issue: ort + Windows ARM64" workaround list (lite / cross-compile / wait-for-stable) with the auto-fix description, including verification steps and a note about the STATICŌåÆDYNAMIC linkage trade-off.
  - **Linkage change:** switches ORT from STATIC (pyke's 290 MB onnxruntime.lib bundled into the exe) to DYNAMIC (Microsoft's small import lib + 12 MB `onnxruntime.dll`). The `ort` crate's `copy-dylibs` default feature places the DLL next to the exe in dev and release builds; tauri-bundler picks it up from `target/release/` for installers.
  - **Validation:** `npm run tauri:dev` (canonical, `desktop-full`) completes end-to-end on aarch64. Logs show `Embedding model AllMiniLML6V2Q loaded successfully`, `mDNS service registered`, `Frontend time-to-interactive: 12848.5 ms`, and the embedding doctrine ingest from `companion::brain::doctrine` runs. The `cpuinfo: Unknown chip model 'Snapdragon X Elite'` warning is from upstream `cpuinfo` and is informational only (not a build error).
  - **Headline:** First reliable fix for the `ort-sys 2.0.0-rc.9` mislabeled-tarball bug on arm64 Windows hosts ŌĆö replaces three workarounds (use lite / cross-compile to x64 / wait for ort 2.0 stable) with a self-healing predev fix that survives `clean:ort`. CI is unaffected (x64 runners, pyke's x64 tarball is correct; the fix is a no-op there). Build-process review identified follow-ups: auto-killing orphan Vite on port 1420, expanding `check-build-cache.mjs` to validate cached binary architecture (currently only checks rustc host-triple drift), and chaining `ensure:ort-cache` after `clean:ort` so the operation always leaves the system in a known-good state.

- **[2026-05-12 14:00 ŌåÆ 15:10] i18n-dead-keys ŌĆö warn-only scanner + 11-section deletion sweep**
  - **Status:** completed (commits `633a38125` scanner, `d193a5588` deletion on master).

  - **Approach:** prefix-match scanner. Reuses `flattenKeys()` shape from `check-coverage.mjs`. Walks `src/**/*.{ts,tsx}` (skips `i18n/`, `__tests__`, `*.test.*`, `*.spec.*`, `generated/`); re-includes 4 sanctioned shape adapters (`useReleasesTranslation`, `useSidebarTranslation`, `useTranslatedError`, `tokenMaps`). Captures `t.<dotted.path>` via regex, plus `tokenLabel(t, '<category>', ŌĆ”)` ŌåÆ `status_tokens.<category>` umbrella, plus `ERROR_KEY_MAP` `keyPrefix:` values parsed out of `useTranslatedError.ts` ŌåÆ `error_registry.<prefix>_{message,suggestion}`. Any en.json key whose path matches or is a prefix of a captured reference is "used". Modes: default (warn, exit 0), `--strict` (exit 1), `--json`, `--full`, `--ignore-prefix=a,b`.
  - **First-run result:** 2152 / 11867 keys flagged unused (18.1%). Worst-offender sections ŌĆö `overview` 531, `agents` 529, `vault` 256, `plugins` 133. Spot-grepped `t.toasts`, `t.composition`, `t.prompt_lab`, `t.alerts`, `t.error_explanation`, `t.cli`, `t.auth` ŌåÆ zero matches in `src/`, confirming the scanner is not generating false positives on whole-section dead-letter cases.

Net: 278 keys removed, 160 files changed, 8697 lines deleted. **Did NOT delete** `alerts, deploy_errors, auth` despite scanner flagging them 100% unused ŌĆö tsc verification caught real references through the `import { en }` Proxy shim in 3 Zustand slices (`authStore`, `alertSlice`, `deployTarget`); restored them from HEAD before commit.

The static scanner doesn't see `en.<section>.<key>` patterns ŌĆö only `t.<section>.<key>`. Discovered the gap by running `npx tsc --noEmit` after the first deletion attempt (3 sections came back with errors). Known follow-up: extend the scanner's reference-capture regex to also match `\ben\.([a-z_][\w.]*)`. Until then, scanner output should be cross-checked with tsc on a regen'd type tree before any deletion.
